\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_ac438e90f6089dd6a944e4bb3dd965fd9}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr@{append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr}}
\index{append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr@{append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int append\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{expr}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_ac438e90f6089dd6a944e4bb3dd965fd9}


Append axis sync. P\-L\-C expression.\par
. 

Add one line to the axis P\-L\-C code.\par
The axis P\-L\-C expression is used for enabling and executing of axes based on mathematical expressions. This is useful when synchronizing axes i.\-e. a slave axis could be enabled and executed at the same time as the master axis.\par
 Example\-: Enable of axis 2 is related to the enable command of axis 1 and 5. The execute command is related to an expression including the execute command for axis 2 and 7.\par
\char`\"{}ax2.\-drv.\-enable\-:=ax1.\-drv.\-enable or ax5.\-drv.\-enable$|$\char`\"{}.\par
 For more syntax help plese view P\-L\-C syntax (\hyperlink{ecmcPLC_8h_ad38da843bcb103392fc2fda9ab4771a0}{set\-P\-L\-C\-Expr()}).\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em expr} & P\-L\-C expression.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set P\-L\-C expression for axes 5 to ax2.\-drv.\-enable\-:=ax1.\-drv.\-enable or ax5.\-drv.\-enable$|$.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-set\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr(5)=ax2.\-drv.\-enable\-:=ax1.\-drv.\-enable or ax5.\-drv.\-enable$|$\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Creates an axis object at index axis\-Index. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

 type = 1 \-: Normal axis (drive, encoder, monitor,pid-\/controller,trajectory).\par
 type = 2 \-: Virtual axis (encoder, monitor, trajectory).\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em drv\-Type} & Type of axis.\par
 type = 0 \-: Simple drive (stepper).\par
 type = 1 \-: D\-S402 drive.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em traj\-Type} & Type of trajectory generator.\par
 type = 0 \-: Trapetzoidal.\par
 type = 1 \-: Jerk limited (s-\/curve, ruckig).\par
\\
\hline

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_ab8878d23f8d435afd2abc4798706c5f0}


Get axis command word.\par
. 

The command word defines different modes of operation for and axis. See fb\-Drive\-Virtual manual for more information.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em value} & axis command word.\par
 value = 0\-: Jog.\par
 value = 1\-: Constant Velocity.\par
 value = 2\-: Relative Positioning.\par
 value = 3\-: Absolute Positioning.\par
 value = 10\-: Homing.\par
 See manual for fb\-Drive\-Virtual for more information.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Get command word for axis 3.\par
\char`\"{}\-Main.\-M3.\-n\-Command?\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

 source = 1 \-: External from transformation expression (synchronization).\par

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a87b8d4dff43a67e035352b9ea98fad8b}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr@{get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr}}
\index{get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr@{get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}const char$\ast$ get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a87b8d4dff43a67e035352b9ea98fad8b}


Get axis encoder transformation expression.\par
. 

The axis transformation expression is used for synchronization of axes. The expression is a mathematical expression describing relation ship between different axes.\par
 Example\-: \char`\"{}out\-:=sin(traj1+enc5)/500;\char`\"{}.\par
 traj1 = trajectory setpoint of axis 1.\par
 enc5 = actual encoder position of axis 5.\par
 out = the encoder setpoint for the current axis (axes\mbox{[}axis\-Index\mbox{]}).\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em error} & Error code.\par
error = 0\-: No error.\par
error $>$ 0\-: Error.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to transformation expression.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Get encoder transformation expression for axes 5.\par
\char`\"{}\-Get\-Axis\-Enc\-Trans\-Expr(5)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

 type = 0 \-: E\-C\-M\-C\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-\_\-\-M\-O\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-M\-A\-L\par
 1\-: E\-C\-M\-C\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-\_\-\-M\-O\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-F\-W\-D (Always forward)\par
 2\-: E\-C\-M\-C\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-\_\-\-M\-O\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-B\-W\-D (always backward)\par
 3\-: E\-C\-M\-C\-\_\-\-M\-O\-D\-\_\-\-M\-O\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-C\-L\-O\-S\-E\-S\-T (closest path)\par
 \\

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a01c465dfef65ac0a46d05507bcc5eb57}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon@{get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}}
\index{get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon@{get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int get\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a01c465dfef65ac0a46d05507bcc5eb57}


Get position lag monitoring enable.\par
. 

The position lag monitoring functionality monitors the difference between the actual position and trajectory generated setpoint position. The motion can be interlocked if the difference exceeds a certain tolerance for a certain number of cycles, see command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a1cda43ec8c0ce0758bf6830df20451ad}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Pos\-Lag\-Time()} and \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a3063908ef15e5ee2b7fa1f29db07a9d3}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Pos\-Lag\-Tol()} for more information.\par
 A big position lag error during a motion could be generated by bad tuning or mechanical issues.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & Enable monitoring.\par
.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par

\end{DoxyReturn}

Get polarity of motion axis interlock from Ether\-C\-A\-T entry.\par
. 

The motion can be interlocked based on an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry. See command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a51cdea4f52b0914715bb3931bc8ec11a}{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Mon()} for more information.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em value} & Polarity external interlock.\par
 0 = N\-C (High is O\-K) Default.\par
 1 = N\-O (Low is O\-K).\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
W\-A\-R\-N\-I\-N\-G\-: If an error is detected, the enable (power) will be removed from the axis. Please always ensure that the power less state is the safe state.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Get external interlock polarity for axis 7.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{get\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}const char$\ast$ get\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a2e2a44ea726c5778b34b331356610244}


Get axis sync. P\-L\-C expression.\par
. 

The axis sync P\-L\-C expression is used for enabling and executing of\par
axes based on mathematical expressions. This is useful when synchronizing\par
axes i.\-e. a slave axis could recive an custom trajatory, other enabled based\textbackslash{} on other axes or ethercat data in the form of mathematical expressions.\par



\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em error} & Error code.\par
error = 0\-: No error.\par
error $>$ 0\-: Error.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to transformation expression.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Get axis sync. P\-L\-C expression for axes 5.\par
\char`\"{}get\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr(5)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a06cdc8ac48b72752d69f62640ebf9148}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr@{get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr}}
\index{get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr@{get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}const char$\ast$ get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a06cdc8ac48b72752d69f62640ebf9148}


Get axis trajectory transformation expression.\par
. 

The axis transformation expression is used for synchronization of axes. The expression is a mathematical expression describing relation ship between different axes.\par
 Example\-: \char`\"{}out\-:=sin(traj1+enc5)/500;\char`\"{}.\par
 traj1 = trajectory setpoint of axis 1.\par
 enc5 = actual encoder position of axis 5.\par
 out = the trajectory setpoint for the current axis (axes\mbox{[}axis\-Index\mbox{]}).\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em error} & Error code.\par
error = 0\-: No error.\par
error $>$ 0\-: Error.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to transformation expression.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Get trajectory transformation expression for axes 5.\par
\char`\"{}\-Get\-Axis\-Traj\-Trans\-Expr(5)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a3289e829b56562432535b317a3f069f4}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv@{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv}}
\index{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv@{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drv (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{slave\-Bus\-Position, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{entry\-Id\-String, }
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{drive\-Entry\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{entry\-Bit\-Index}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a3289e829b56562432535b317a3f069f4}


Links an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry to the drive object of the axis at axis\-Index. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em slave\-Bus\-Position} & Position of the Ether\-C\-A\-T slave on the bus.\par
 slave\-Bus\-Position = -\/1\-: Used to address the simulation slave. Only two entries are configured, \char`\"{}\-Z\-E\-R\-O\char`\"{} with default value 0 and \char`\"{}\-O\-N\-E\char`\"{} with default value 1.\par
 slave\-Bus\-Position = 0..65535\-: Addressing of normal Ether\-C\-A\-T slaves\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em entry\-Id\-String} & String for addressing purpose (see command \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Ec\-Add\-Entry\-Complete() for more information\char`\"{}). If left blank drive\-Entry\-Index == 3 or4, the corresponding functionality will be disabled.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Index of axis to link to.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em drive\-Entry\-Index} & Index of drive objects entry list.\par
 drive\-Entry\-Index = 0\-: Amplifier enable (output).\par
 drive\-Entry\-Index = 1\-: Velocity setpoint (output).\par
 drive\-Entry\-Index = 2\-: Amplifier enabled (input).\par
 drive\-Entry\-Index = 3\-: Brake (output).\par
 Brake func will be enabled.\par
 drive\-Entry\-Index = 4\-: Reduce torque (output). Reduce torque func will be enabled.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em entry\-Bit\-Index} & Bit index of Ether\-C\-A\-T entry to use.\par
 entry\-Bit\-Index = -\/1\-: All bits of the entry will be used.\par
 entry\-Bit\-Index = 0..64\-: Only the selected bit will be used.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example 1\-: Link an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry configured as \char`\"{}\-V\-E\-L\-O\-C\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-S\-E\-T\char`\"{} in slave 3 as velocity setpoint entry for the drive object of axis 5.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drive(3,\-V\-E\-L\-O\-C\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-S\-E\-T,5,1,-\/1)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c\par
 Example 2\-: Link bit 0 of an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry configured as \char`\"{}\-S\-T\-M\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-T\-R\-O\-L\char`\"{} in slave 3 as enable amplifier output entry for the drive object of axis 5.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drive(3,\-S\-T\-M\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-T\-R\-O\-L,5,0,0)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c\par
 Example 3\-: If a drive have no feedback for enable, a simulation slave and entry can be used. The simulation Ether\-C\-A\-T slave can be addressed with a slave\-Bus\-Index of -\/1. The simulation slave contains two entries, \char`\"{}\-Z\-E\-R\-O\char`\"{} with default value zero and \char`\"{}\-O\-N\-E\char`\"{} with default value set to 1.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Drive(-\/1,\-O\-N\-E,5,0,0)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Links an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry to the monitor object of the axis at axis\-Index\par
. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em slave\-Bus\-Position} & Position of the Ether\-C\-A\-T slave on the bus.\par
 slave\-Bus\-Position = -\/1\-: Used to address the simulation slave. Only two entries are configured, \char`\"{}\-Z\-E\-R\-O\char`\"{} with default value 0 and \char`\"{}\-O\-N\-E\char`\"{} with default value 1.\par
 slave\-Bus\-Position = 0..65535\-: Addressing of normal Ether\-C\-A\-T slaves.\par

 \\

Example 1\-: Link an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry configured as \char`\"{}\-I\-N\-P\-U\-T\-\_\-0\char`\"{} in slave 1 as forward limit switch entry for the monitor object of axis 5.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Monitor(1,\char`\"{}I\-N\-P\-U\-T\-\_\-0\char`\"{},5,1,0)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c\par
 Example 2\-: If an axis is not equipped with limit switches the entries for limit switches needs to be linked to the simulation entries. The simulation slave contains two entries, \char`\"{}\-Z\-E\-R\-O\char`\"{} with default value zero and \char`\"{}\-O\-N\-E\char`\"{} with default value set to 1.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Monitor(-\/1,\-O\-N\-E,5,1,0)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Links an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry to the an axis object for status output\par
. 

The output will be high when the axis object is without error code and otherwise zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em slave\-Index} & Position of the Ether\-C\-A\-T slave on the bus.\par
 slave\-Index = -\/1\-: Used to address the simulation slave. Only two entries are configured, \char`\"{}\-Z\-E\-R\-O\char`\"{} with default value 0 and \char`\"{}\-O\-N\-E\char`\"{} with default value 1.\par
 slave\-Index = 0..65535\-: Addressing of normal Ether\-C\-A\-T slaves.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em entry\-Id\-String} & String for addressing purpose (see command \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Ec\-Add\-Entry\-Complete() for more information\char`\"{}).\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Index of axis.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example 1\-: Link an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry configured as \char`\"{}\-O\-U\-T\-P\-U\-T\-\_\-0\char`\"{} in slave 1 as status output for axis with index 2.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Allow commands from P\-L\-Cs.\par

An axis can receive commands from P\-L\-Cs (see P\-L\-C syntax). However, the axis must be allow to receive these commands, see command set\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Expr() for more information.\par

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a58fc7be26fe1d7690c9f277fdeced655}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data@{set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data}}
\index{set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data@{set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int set\-Axis\-Cmd\-Data (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a58fc7be26fe1d7690c9f277fdeced655}


Set axis command data word.\par
. 

The command data word is an argument linked to the axis command. See fb\-Drive\-Virtual manual for more information.\par
A new command will be triggered with a positive edge on the b\-Execute flag.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & Axis command data word.\par
 The command data word have different meaning depending on the command word.\par
 Command word = 1 (Move velocity)\-: \par
 Command data 0\-: Move Velocity\par
 Command word = 2 (Relative positioning)\-: \par
 Command data 0\-: Move relative\par
 Command word = 3 (absolute positioning)\-: \par
 Command data 0\-: Default absolute positioning\par
 Command Data 1\-: Go to start position of trajectory generator external transformation expressions. This is useful to avoid jumps during start phase when absolute synchronizing.\par
 Command word = 10 (Referencing to f\-Home\-Position)\-:\par
 Command Data 0\-: Simplest homing sequence. The actual position of the encoder will be set to f\-Home\-Position. Command Data 1\-: Ref. on low limit switch.\par
 Command Data 2\-: Ref. on high limit switch.\par
 Command Data 3\-: Ref. on home sensor via low limit switch.\par
 Command Data 4\-: Ref. on home sensor via high limit switch.\par
 Command Data 5\-: Ref. on center of home sensor via low limit switch.\par
 Command Data 6\-: Ref. on center of home sensor via high limit switch.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Prepare homing sequence 3 at next positive edge of execute for axis 3 (two command needed).\par
\char`\"{}\-Main.\-M3.\-n\-Command=10\char`\"{} //\-Set homing. Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par
\char`\"{}\-Main.\-M3.\-n\-Cmd\-Data=3\char`\"{} //\-Set homing sequence. Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\hyperlink{todo__todo000038}{Todo}]"Twin\-C\-A\-T syntax. Needs to be changed.\par
 \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\item[{int}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a1047c398e89663a628995435105e1a70}


Set axis command word.\par
. 

The command word defines different modes of operation for and axis. See fb\-Drive\-Virtual manual for more information.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & axis command word.\par
 value = 0\-: Jog.\par
 value = 1\-: Constant Velocity.\par
 value = 2\-: Relative Positioning.\par
 value = 3\-: Absolute Positioning.\par
 value = 10\-: Homing.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set command word to absolute positioning for axis 4.\par
\char`\"{}\-Main.\-M4.\-n\-Command=3\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{enable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_af1af455e057dfed49b4f33c4ec3fe598}


Set enable of brake.\par
. 

The brake output will follow the amplifier enable state of the drive. The brake is high when amplifier enable is high and low when amplifier enable is low.\par
 Note\-: Delays are can be configured with\-:\par
 -\/set\-Axis\-Drv\-Brake\-Open\-Delay\-Time() \par
 -\/set\-Axis\-Drv\-Brake\-Close\-Ahead\-Time() \par
 Note\-: A valid Ether\-C\-A\-T entry must be linked to the drive objects brake entry in order to work like intended.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & Brake enable.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Enable brake for axis 3.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Drv\-Brake\-Enable(3,1)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

\item[{int}]{bits}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a2c863cf31139c4b72f96c40ccde3bb4a}


Set encoder register bit count for absolute data.\par
. 

This setting is used for homing of partly absolute encoders\par
like resolvers (single turn absolute). The data is always\par
considered to be located at the least significant bits\par
of the encoder data (masked). See \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a30e6a803febf84430eff63ad417becec}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits()} and\par
\hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a43564186dab00e680cb2afb1cb7c9dbf}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Raw\-Mask()} for more information.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em bits} & Encoder register bit count for absolute data.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set encoder absolute bit count to 10 for axis 3.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Enc\-Abs\-Bits(3,10)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a30e6a803febf84430eff63ad417becec}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits@{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits}}
\index{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits@{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{bits}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a30e6a803febf84430eff63ad417becec}


Set encoder register bit count.\par
. 

The bit count is used to handle over/under flow.\par
 \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\-: The bits will be considered to be the least significant\par
 of the encoder data area. The raw encoder mask will therefore\par
 be set to 2$^\wedge$bits-\/1 (see \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a43564186dab00e680cb2afb1cb7c9dbf}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Raw\-Mask()} for more info). If\par
 bits need to be filtered away then use \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a43564186dab00e680cb2afb1cb7c9dbf}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Raw\-Mask()} command\par
 instead.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em bits} & Encoder register bit count.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set encoder bit count to 16 for axis 3.\par
 \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits(3,16)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Set encoder raw data mask.\par
. 

Mask to filter Encoder data from encoder 64bit data\par
Also calculates bit-\/count of encoder data. If this function \par
is used then the \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a30e6a803febf84430eff63ad417becec}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits()} should N\-O\-T be used since\par
. \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a30e6a803febf84430eff63ad417becec}{set\-Axis\-Enc\-Bits()} also calculates and sets the a raw-\/mask\par
(but based on all data located on the least significant bits).\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raw\-Mask} & Encoder raw mask.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set encoder mask to 0x\-F\-F\-F\-F for axis 3.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Enc\-Raw\-Mask(3,0x\-F\-F\-F\-F)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

Set off cam referencing/homing velocity setpoint.\par
. 

This velocity setpoint is only used during homing sequence when the reference switch already have been found. See command \char`\"{}get\-Axis\-Home\-Vel\-Towards\-Cam()\char`\"{} for more information.\par
Normally the off cam velocity setpoint is lower than the Towards cam setpoint since the accuracy of homing is depending on how accurate the signal edge of the reference switch can be identified.\par

 Note\-: The \char`\"{}at target\char`\"{} functionality needs to be enabled by the command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a652ab525bb085e909a6cd48ba39ec0e3}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-At\-Target\-Mon()}.\par

. 

Set maximum allowed controller output for an axis.\par

 \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
W\-A\-R\-N\-I\-N\-G\-: If an error is detected, the enable (power) will be removed from the axis. Please always ensure that the power less state is the safe state.\par

Enable controller output high limit monitoring.\par
. 

The controller output high limit monitoring functionality monitors the controller output. The motion can be interlocked if the controller output exceeds a certain tolerance, see command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a834918edc6506892dde63f26ee7d75d1}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Cntrl\-Out\-H\-L()} for more information.\par
 A high controller output during a motion could be generated by bad tuning or mechanical issues.\par
 \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
W\-A\-R\-N\-I\-N\-G\-: If an error is detected, the enable (power) will be removed from the axis. Please always ensure that the power less state is the safe state.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\

 \\

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Disable controller output high limit monitoring for axis 2.\par

\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_ac946a392e16e28760dbb96033b41f33f}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon@{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}}
\index{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon@{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}!ecmcMotion.h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_ac946a392e16e28760dbb96033b41f33f}


Enable position lag monitoring.\par
. 

The position lag monitoring functionality monitors the difference between the actual position and trajectory generated setpoint position. The motion can be interlocked if the difference exceeds a certain tolerance for a certain number of cycles, see command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a1cda43ec8c0ce0758bf6830df20451ad}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Pos\-Lag\-Time()} and \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a3063908ef15e5ee2b7fa1f29db07a9d3}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Pos\-Lag\-Tol()} for more information.\par
 A big position lag error during a motion could be generated by bad tuning or mechanical issues.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & monitoring enabled.\par
.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Disable position lag monitoring for axis 2.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Lag\-Mon(2,0)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

. 

The motion can be interlocked based on an Ether\-C\-A\-T entry. See command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_a51cdea4f52b0914715bb3931bc8ec11a}{link\-Ec\-Entry\-To\-Axis\-Mon()} for more information.\par

\\

 1 = N\-O (Low is O\-K).\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
W\-A\-R\-N\-I\-N\-G\-: If an error is detected, the enable (power) will be removed from the axis. Please always ensure that the power less state is the safe state.\par

\item[{int}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_af5a02717425e252c978b7830c6578379}


Set velocity monitoring interlock delay for drive.\par
. 

The over speed interlock for the drive can be delayed in order ensure that encoder noise reulsting in a high velocity will not interlock motion. If the overspeed interlock is still active after this amount of cycles the drive will be interlocked and the amplifier will be turned off.\par
 Note\-: The maximum velocity monitoring needs to be enabled with the command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_aae0f40ec66aa421dd0172fd0e29f2746}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Max\-Vel()}.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & Delay cycles.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set drive over speed interlock delay to 10 cycles for axis 4.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Mon\-Max\-Vel\-Drive\-I\-L\-Delay(4,10)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}

Set velocity monitoring interlock delay for trajectory.\par
. 

The over speed interlock for the trajectory generator can be delayed in order ensure that encoder noise reulsting in a high velocity will not interlock motion. If the overspeed interlock is still active after this amount of cycles the trajectory generator will be interlocked and velocity will be ramped down to stand still.\par
 Note\-: The maximum velocity monitoring needs to be enabled with the command \hyperlink{ecmcMotion_8h_aae0f40ec66aa421dd0172fd0e29f2746}{set\-Axis\-Mon\-Enable\-Max\-Vel()}.\par

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{axis\-Index, }
\item[{int}]{enable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ecmcMotion_8h_a95f135fc54382fcbc74ec2f65558e916}


Enables/disables velocity filter of external setpoint.\par
. 

This filter is needed in order to have a smoth feedforward value when\par
 reciving setpoints form an P\-L\-C. If filter is disabled the velocity will\par
 be calculated based on the last two postion values recived from P\-L\-C. In many\par
 cases this will result in a \char`\"{}unstable signal\char`\"{} depending onresoltions of the\par
 values involved in the calculation. Using a filter will smoth the velocity\par
 feed forward value and will thereby result in a smoother motion.\par
 \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\-: This filter is only enabled when the axis recives setpoin ts from an P\-L\-C.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em enable} & enable filter.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Enable velocity filter for external setpoint position for axis 5. "Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Traj\-Vel\-Filter\-Enable(5,1) //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ecmcMotion_8h_a6203c5de2751aa8c2035faa41e8208e5}{\index{ecmc\-Motion.\-h@{ecmc\-Motion.\-h}!set\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Traj\-Vel\-Filter\-Size@{set\-Axis\-P\-L\-C\-Traj\-Vel\-Filter\-Size}}

Set size of external trajectory velocity filter.\par
. 

Sets the size of the filter for velocity from \char`\"{}external\char`\"{} P\-L\-C code.\par
 This filter is needed in order to have a smoth feedforward value when\par
 reciving setpoints form an P\-L\-C. If filter is disabled the velocity will\par
 be calculated based on the last two postion values recived from P\-L\-C. In many\par
 cases this will result in a \char`\"{}unstable signal\char`\"{} depending onresoltions of the\par
 values involved in the calculation. Using a filter will smoth the velocity\par
 feed forward value and will thereby rresult in a smoother motion.\par
 \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\-: This filter is only enabled when the axis recives setpoin ts from an P\-L\-C.\par
 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

Set sequence timeout time in seconds.\par
. 

The motion sequences (mainly related to homing) can be aborted if not finalized within a certain time. This is to prevent that the motion control hangs in one sequence. This could happen if the reference switch for some reason is not encountered.\par

Set axis target velocity setpoint.\par
. 

The target velocity is the desired velocity of a motion.\par
Note\-: The actual velocity can be higher than this setpoint.\par
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em axis\-Index} & Axis index.\par
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & Target velocity setpoint.\par
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if success or otherwise an error code.\par
 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Example\-: Set target velocity setpoint for axis 3 to 55.\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Vel(3,55)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par
 

Example\-: Set target velocity setpoint for axis 3 to 55 in\par
\char`\"{}\-Twin\-C\-A\-T\char`\"{} syntax.\par
\char`\"{}\-Main.\-M3.\-f\-Velocity=55\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par
 

The \char`\"{}\-Cfg\-Set\-Axis\-Vel\-Acc\-Dec\-Time()\char`\"{} Command can be used to set\par
velocity, acceleration and decelartion simultaneously\par
Acceleration and deceleration are defined by time to reach target velocity\par
Syntax\-: \char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Vel\-Acc\-Dec\-Time(axis\-Index,target\-Vel,time\-To\-Vel)\char`\"{}

Example\-: Set target velocity setpoint for axis 3 to 55 and time to reach target velocity to 2s (acc and dec will be set to the same\par
value).\par
\char`\"{}\-Cfg.\-Set\-Axis\-Vel\-Acc\-Dec\-Time(3,55,2)\char`\"{} //\-Command string to ecmc\-Cmd\-Parser.\-c.\par

\end{DoxyNote}
